Reproduced that GNU `env` combined short-option forms `env -vu CLAUDE_GOAL_DB python claude_goal.py stop-hook`, `env -vC DIR python claude_goal.py stop-hook`, `/usr/bin/env -vS "python -u" claude_goal.py stop-hook`, and structured `["-vu", "CLAUDE_GOAL_DB", "python", ...]` were not counted as `/goal` Stop hooks. Verified actual execution with Git for Windows `env.exe`: `-vu` unset the env var and executed Python, `-vC` changed directory and executed Python, and `-vS` split `python -u` and executed Python; all wrote the marker through the target script with `stop-hook`. Root cause was that `env` wrapper detection only consumed separate `-v`, `-u`, `-C`, and `-S` tokens, not GNU combined short-option tokens. `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` and `goal/scripts/install_goal.py` now consume reproduced `-v+[uC]` wrapper operands and route `-v+S` through the existing split-string launcher path, without treating `env -vu ... echo claude_goal.py stop-hook` as a goal hook. `tests/test_claude_goal.py` and `tests/test_install_goal.py` cover shell-form, structured, migration, and false-positive echo variants. |

## Rotation 2026-06-10 (archived addenda older than 2026-06-03)

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Date | 2026-06-10 |
| Tool | Codex |
| Work | **claude-goal env -i home-less Stop-hook import fix**. Continued the user-requested `/goal` autonomous debugging loop inside the separate `claude-goal/` subrepo while preserving root dirty-handoff WIP and without staging, commit, push, revert, `update_goal`, product/browser edits, or Hanwoo T-251 retry. 0-step current root inventory was rerun first: root workspace remains blocked on `dirty_worktree_handoff_current`, user-owned Hanwoo T-251, unpushed current-head Actions, Blind-to-X dirty handoff, and incomplete launch audit; no root product edit was started. In the nested repo, reproduced a real Stop-hook crash using Git for Windows `env.exe -i CLAUDE_GOAL_DB=... CLAUDE_GOAL_SESSION_ID=... <absolute python> goal/scripts/claude_goal.py stop-hook`: before the fix the process exited `1` at import with `RuntimeError: Could not determine home directory` from `Path.home()`. Root cause: top-level path constants used eager `os.environ.get(..., Path.home() / ...)` defaults, so `Path.home()` was evaluated even when `CLAUDE_GOAL_DB` was explicitly supplied in a home-less environment. `goal/scripts/claude_goal.py` now resolves env-provided paths lazily, derives `STATE_DIR` from explicit `CLAUDE_GOAL_DB` when no `CLAUDE_GOAL_HOME` exists, and falls back to state-dir-relative settings/skill/commands paths only when `Path.home()` is unavailable. `tests/test_claude_goal.py` adds `test_stop_hook_uses_explicit_db_when_home_environment_is_missing`. |
| Next Priorities | Verification passed: direct `env.exe -i` repro now returns Stop-hook block JSON (`decision=block`, objective present, stderr empty), focused isolated-env pytest (`1 passed`), related focused pytest (`3 passed`), full nested suite (`386 passed` after format), Ruff check, source-scoped Ruff format check (`goal tests`), `py_compile`, `git diff --check` with LF/CRLF warnings only, and nested `code_review_graph detect-changes` risk `0.00`. `env --list-signal-handling` was checked as the next candidate and is **not** a bug: it executes the command and both runtime/installer detectors already return true for shell and structured forms. Continued the nested `claude-goal/` stop-hook detector loop after the cmd amp-tail segment fix while preserving concurrent root auto-research WIP. Reproduced a Windows `cmd` false negative where `cmd.exe /d /s /c "echo ready&python .../claude_goal.py stop-hook"` and structured `/d /s /c` tail `echo ready&python .../claude_goal.py stop-hook` both executed a temporary marker hook (`rc=0`, marker written), while doctor and installer detection returned false. Both detector copies now split unquoted, unescaped single `&` inside cmd tail tokens into operator parts, while leaving quoted tokens, escaped `^&`, and `&&` unsplit, then reuse the existing segment, `call`, and Python launcher checks. Tests add positive shell/structured glued `echo ready&python` and `echo ready&call python` coverage plus negative shell/structured glued `echo ready&echo` coverage. |
